This evening they<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> killed and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9427' title='baked'>baked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>. We <a href='../subjects/9428' title='boiled'>boiled</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> and <a href='../subjects/9429' title='stewed'>stewed</a> <a href='../subjects/9430' title='fruit'>fruit</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I washed a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7569' title='garments'>garments</a> &amp; a lot of olde<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/199' title='stockings'>stockings</a>. Ben &amp; Josie <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> night and morning. The<span class='line-break'> </span> children <a href='../subjects/9421' title='played games'>played games</a> tonigh.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has gone to <a href='../subjects/9392' title='Strait Stone'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to meet at the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>. He went <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse back</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The mud is so bad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1939">
<h3><a name="page-1939">Sunday, February 12, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/9260' title='Rained'>Rained</a> a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all stayed at home but<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a>. He went to <a href='../subjects/9431' title='Dr Owens'>Dr Owens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and spent the day with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9432' title='Stewart'>Stewart</a>. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> went with <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> to <a href='../subjects/7225' title='Steven Davis'>Steven Davis</a> s<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening to get his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a>. They come home a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> dark. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/9427' title='baked'>baked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9324' title='breat'>breat</a> &amp; made <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> supper. Today has bin one<span class='line-break'> </span> lonesome dreary day. The <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a><span class='line-break'> </span> are so bad that no one cant<span class='line-break'> </span> get a bout much. Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a> this morning &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie milked by her self to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. I wish I could see <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children once more.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1940">
<h3><a name="page-1940">Monday, February 13, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Hattie Gilbert<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/9412' title='Mr Booker'>Mr Booker</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I am glad he<span class='line-break'> </span> is back.  I have no <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a><span class='line-break'> </span> fit to write with.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> today.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1941">
<h3><a name="page-1941">Tuesday, February 14, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/49' title='Rain'>Rain</a> tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>hail</a>. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/9359' title='cut'>cut</a> in <span class='line-break'> </span> the woods today. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9241' title='churned'>churned</a> and washed dishes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9366' title='Marvin'>Marvin</a> come today. He eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner with us. He got his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> from <a href='../subjects/9433' title='Bookers'>Bookers</a> and <a href='../subjects/7620' title='lard'>lard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from here. I am glad for<span class='line-break'> </span> him that it is at home. He<span class='line-break'> </span> said that his folks was bad<span class='line-break'> </span> off with <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>. I do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> that they may soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a letter from <a href='../subjects/9434' title='Julia Fergerson'>Julia <span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> today. Was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to hear from her. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> got a valentine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1942">
<h3><a name="page-1942">Wednesday, February 15, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/9351' title='bad'>bad</a> day. It has <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9260' title='rained'>rained</a> nearly all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The trees are covered in <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> and lots of limbs<span class='line-break'> </span> has broke off. The weeping<span class='line-break'> </span> willow at the spring fell<span class='line-break'> </span> over this evening. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> could not work out at <span class='line-break'> </span> anything. Ben <a href='../subjects/9390' title='mended'>mended</a> up<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/9436' title='chairs'>chairs</a>. Jim <a href='../subjects/9390' title='mended'>mended</a><span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I am uneasy that he<span class='line-break'> </span> is going to be <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a>. I am<span class='line-break'> </span> uneasy a bout them all.<span class='line-break'> </span> The weather is so bad. I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that God will keep them<span class='line-break'> </span> well and able to stand up under it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1943">
<h3><a name="page-1943">Thursday, February 16, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/9437' title='Snowed'>Snowed</a> again last night and<span class='line-break'> </span> have not <a href='../subjects/9438' title='thawed'>thawed</a> but very little<span class='line-break'> </span> allday. Today it is a very bad time.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a> today. I am not <span class='line-break'> </span> going out much. We <a href='../subjects/9439' title='dressed'>dressed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> today and <a href='../subjects/9373' title='cooked'>cooked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> one. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the weather was two bad for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a>. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9204' title='Mabel'>Mabel</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>. I think <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> feels better than he did<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday. I know I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> he does. I am sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> myself and every boddy<span class='line-break'> </span> esle [crossed out] else. I want to hear<span class='line-break'> </span> from all of my children<span class='line-break'> </span> and grand children. Do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> that the weather will get good.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1944">
<h3><a name="page-1944">Friday, February 17, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/443' title='colde'>colde</a> day. Partly <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> did not melt but very<span class='line-break'> </span> little to day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9352' title='sawed'>sawed</a> up the weeping willow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today the weather is so <a href='../subjects/9351' title='bad'>bad</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that they cant do much. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> made some <a href='../subjects/9440' title='foot stools'>foot stools</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Walker Haris [(Col)?coloured man] brought<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/9436' title='chairs'>chairs</a> that he had to put<span class='line-break'> </span> bottoms in and a <a href='../subjects/9441' title='basket'>basket</a><span class='line-break'> </span> good but rough. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to school. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/9442' title='croupy'>croupy</a> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think he is better though.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a letter from <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie today. They are all a <span class='line-break'> </span> bout but not well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1945">
<h3><a name="page-1945">Saturday, February 18, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day most of the day and<span class='line-break'> </span> some warmer and so much mud<span class='line-break'> </span> that roads is all most impasable.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9443' title='Miss Wille Wooding'>Miss Wille Wooding</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with us. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and it was a good one.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/9265' title='Renan'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They couldnt get a <a href='../subjects/9444' title='box'>box</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> would do for a box to pack meat.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh all of the children has<span class='line-break'> </span> bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> is <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a>. Bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sick all day. I am not well<span class='line-break'> </span> but I hope I may be better<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning. I have bin<span class='line-break'> </span> miserable this evening. So much<span class='line-break'> </span> to do and I am not able<span class='line-break'> </span> to help much. I would like<span class='line-break'> </span> to help some. I do so much hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that the children may be better in the morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1946">
<h3><a name="page-1946">Sunday, February 19, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day. We all<span class='line-break'> </span> stayed at home. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was lookin up <a href='../subjects/9445' title='plank'>plank</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for a <a href='../subjects/9444' title='box'>box</a> to put his met<span class='line-break'> </span> in. The children has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin up to day. All of them<span class='line-break'> </span> has bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>. I have<span class='line-break'> </span> bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have <a href='../subjects/9373' title='cooked'>cooked</a> what we<span class='line-break'> </span> eat today &amp; <a href='../subjects/9241' title='churned'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7966' title='Mrs Booker'>Mrs Booker</a> come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Oh the bad weather.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1947">
<h3><a name="page-1947">Monday, February 20, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span><a href='../subjects/9446' title='trimmed'>trimmed</a> up some <a href='../subjects/9447' title='apple trees'>apple trees</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> come today. I<span class='line-break'> </span>was glad to see her. I had a<span class='line-break'> </span><a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/9270' title='Carrie'>Carrie</a>. Was glad to<span class='line-break'> </span>hear from her &amp; them all.<span class='line-break'> </span>I am <a href='../subjects/9449' title='not well'>not well</a> and <a href='../subjects/9204' title='Mabel'>Mabel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>is crying and going on so that<span class='line-break'> </span>I am tempted to go off some<span class='line-break'> </span>where. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> has <a href='../subjects/9450' title='whipped'>whipped</a> her<span class='line-break'> </span>more than she ever did in <span class='line-break'> </span>her life. Gess she needs it<span class='line-break'> </span>but I can hardly stand<span class='line-break'> </span>it. <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span>bin up all day today.<span class='line-break'> </span>I do hope that times will get<span class='line-break'> </span>better here soon. If they dont<span class='line-break'> </span>I would go some where if I knowed<span class='line-break'> </span>where to go.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1948">
<h3><a name="page-1948">Tuesday, February 21, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day but no <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> helped <a href='../subjects/9370' title='Johnson'>Johnson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/9451' title='phone line'>phone line</a>. They eat<span class='line-break'> </span> with Johnson. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> here. <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> <a href='../subjects/9240' title='ironed'>ironed</a> a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have set by the fire all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. I have a <a href='../subjects/9452' title='bad cold'>bad cold</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening. The come<span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come. I had bin<span class='line-break'> </span> wanting to see some of <span class='line-break'> </span> our folks so long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today 57 years ago I was <span class='line-break'> </span> married. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. Tonight he has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a>. Two of <a href='../subjects/9453' title='Less Booker'>Less<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker</a>s children is there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1949">
<h3><a name="page-1949">Wednesday, February 22, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9394' title='good'>good</a> day. The best that has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> this year. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/9451' title='phone line'>phone line</a> a gain today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I have helped<span class='line-break'> </span> a round some today. Hattie &amp; Elic<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today. <a href='../subjects/9454' title='George Blair Jr'>George Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> Jr</a>. come here this morning for<span class='line-break'> </span> his mothers <a href='../subjects/9455' title='over shoes'>over shoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9270' title='Carrie'>Carrie</a> &amp; her children except<span class='line-break'> </span> Paul come a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> We were glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> The baby has fattened up and<span class='line-break'> </span> is so pretty. I miss them<span class='line-break'> </span> more than i can tell. I do <span class='line-break'> </span> hope that the roads may<span class='line-break'> </span> get good soon. The boys <span class='line-break'> </span> have some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> to market<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1950">

A <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> passed<span class='line-break'> </span> here today. The first one<span class='line-break'> </span> in some time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; tonight. </p>

</div>

<div id="page-1952">
<h3><a name="page-1952">Saturday, February 25, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9394' title='good'>good</a> day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to see his folks. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8444' title='Benjami Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> trimed on the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Helped <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a> <a href='../subjects/7641' title='feed cutting'>cut</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some logs for sills. <span class='line-break'> </span> Otto Blair and Sollie<span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/9433' title='Bookers'>Bookers</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to Normans<span class='line-break'> </span> and staid until bed <span class='line-break'> </span> time. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> is <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a gain today. <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> said a wake until<span class='line-break'> </span> ten oclock tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8444' title='Benjami Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got home<span class='line-break'> </span> at eleven. I am writing<span class='line-break'> </span> in <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> room tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they all may feel<span class='line-break'> </span> better soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1953">
<h3><a name="page-1953">Sunday, February 26, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  Rain this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have bin at home all day. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie milked. I got breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; dinner. Josie washed the<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes after dinner. We had <span class='line-break'> </span> fried chicken for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie bathed the children<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; dressed them. They have<span class='line-break'> </span> worried us to [death] with the<span class='line-break'> </span> fuss they keep up. I have thought<span class='line-break'> </span> of Carrie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> so often. I wish I could<span class='line-break'> </span> be with them a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel dont want to go<span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep and is crying.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh I feel like I will<span class='line-break'> </span> be so glad when the <span class='line-break'> </span> weather is better. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1954">
<h3><a name="page-1954">Monday, February 27, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben loaded on<span class='line-break'> </span> his &amp; Jims tobacco this morning,<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr John Tucker carried<span class='line-break'> </span> it to Danville.  The roads<span class='line-break'> </span> is very rough.  Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker helped Ben handle <span class='line-break'> </span> his tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry &amp; Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Nellie come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I was glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> they did. Oscar Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> brought them from Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> We miss Ben tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is the first time he<span class='line-break'> </span> has been a way in a long<span class='line-break'> </span> time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1955">
<h3><a name="page-1955">Tuesday, February 28, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. Ben was in<span class='line-break'> </span> Danville. Solde the last tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> that they had. Did not get much<span class='line-break'> </span> for it. Ben got home OK<span class='line-break'> </span> a little after dark. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> shucked some corn and fed<span class='line-break'> </span> the stalks to the cows.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin come and eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with us. I was so glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> see him.  Josie ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> Nell ironed some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry is reading. He sleeps<span class='line-break'> </span> in my room now that Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> is home. Anna Callans (col)[coloured]<span class='line-break'> </span> come here and wanted to <span class='line-break'> </span> rent a house. I am sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> for her but dont want her<span class='line-break'> </span> here.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1956">
<h3><a name="page-1956">Wednesday, March  1, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day. Hailed &amp; snowed<span class='line-break'> </span> and rained all day. Hailing<span class='line-break'> </span> now 8 oclock at night.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks fed the<span class='line-break'> </span> stock and made fires. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie milked. I churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner. We had<span class='line-break'> </span> turnip salit &amp; poached<span class='line-break'> </span> eggs.  Nellie &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> brought the sallit from<span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham. We were very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of it. Henry &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has cried a lot<span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning. Was<span class='line-break'> </span> better all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie was complaining<span class='line-break'> </span> all evening. Hope she will<span class='line-break'> </span> soon be teethed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1957">
<h3><a name="page-1957">Thursday, March  2, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day. The ground was<span class='line-break'> </span> covered with snow &amp; ice and it<span class='line-break'> </span> rained most of the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim could not work at<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing much. Jim kept a<span class='line-break'> </span> good fire at the dining room.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Renan late<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. He went horse back.<span class='line-break'> </span> He carried Kate Harvey some<span class='line-break'> </span> quilting frames. Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. I cooked the break<span class='line-break'> </span> fast &amp; churned and killed <span class='line-break'> </span> a chicken and d[r]essed it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie cooked the dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and made ice cream. We<span class='line-break'> </span> all did enjoy it. Josie got a<span class='line-break'> </span> letter from Carrie. I got<span class='line-break'> </span> one from Effie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> and three of their pictures.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1958">
<h3><a name="page-1958">Friday, March  3, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Some snow on the ground<span class='line-break'> </span> yet. Jim &amp; Ben sawed<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood in the woods. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Nellie and Josie caught<span class='line-break'> </span> some chickens to night. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Renan after a crate<span class='line-break'> </span> he wanted. He walked and<span class='line-break'> </span> toated it home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got dinner. She is <span class='line-break'> </span> not well and I see trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout her. I am not doing<span class='line-break'> </span> much and it hurts me<span class='line-break'> </span> for her to have so much to do.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie wants to go home in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning. I am afraid it<span class='line-break'> </span> will be raining. Hope not. The<span class='line-break'> </span> roads is so bad that they will<span class='line-break'> </span> have to go on a waggon if they go.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1959">
<h3><a name="page-1959">Saturday, March  4, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning. Rained most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the night. The trees was covered<span class='line-break'> </span> in ice this morning. Not heavy enough<span class='line-break'> </span> to brake them. Josie baked a cake<span class='line-break'> </span> for Nellie. Nellie dressed a<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken to take home with<span class='line-break'> </span> her. I let her have some<span class='line-break'> </span> butter. They borrowed Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers buggy and started<span class='line-break'> </span> home a bout two oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> in the evening. It has not<span class='line-break'> </span> rained since they left. I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope that they got to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> in time to take the train.<span class='line-break'> </span> At this time the roads is<span class='line-break'> </span> very bad. None of feel good<span class='line-break'> </span> and the wether is depressing<span class='line-break'> </span> on a well person. We should<span class='line-break'> </span> be thankful of the good that we have.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1960">
<h3><a name="page-1960">Sunday, March  5, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. I got breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> and washed the dishes &amp; churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie milked the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made ice cream. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> helped her. Then she baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a cake. It was very nice.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Role Hubbards.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not get home until<span class='line-break'> </span> late. Found them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Grace Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> and Lottie Kellie &amp; Ruth<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker they had four little<span class='line-break'> </span> children with them. Hugh<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come and played<span class='line-break'> </span> with Henry. Josie milked<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight &amp; fed everything.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1961">
<h3><a name="page-1961">Monday, March  6, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna. Carried some eggs<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; chicken and butter.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bought ship stuff &amp; brand<span class='line-break'> </span> for the cows. Sugar &amp; molasses<span class='line-break'> </span> for the folks. Jim come home<span class='line-break'> </span> from Chatham. He brought<span class='line-break'> </span> sallit. We are glad to get<span class='line-break'> </span> it. Mrs Car come today. We<span class='line-break'> </span> was glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George Blairs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dena and I worked on her<span class='line-break'> </span> quilt. It will be very pretty<span class='line-break'> </span> when she finishes it. Denia<span class='line-break'> </span> and Cordie were coming to<span class='line-break'> </span> see us if I had not went<span class='line-break'> </span> there. Hope they will come<span class='line-break'> </span> soon. Denia &amp; Isla had washed<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1962">
<h3><a name="page-1962">Tuesday, March  7, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning. Clear tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> and the wind blowing<span class='line-break'> </span> and colde. Jim &amp; Ben did<span class='line-break'> </span> not do any work this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening they cut some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I got dinner. We<span class='line-break'> </span> had turnip greens &amp; potatoe<span class='line-break'> </span> sallid. Henry and Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Booker come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening. She<span class='line-break'> </span> swapped some eggs to set.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car churned for<span class='line-break'> </span> me this morning. Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> is not sleepy to night<span class='line-break'> </span> but I am.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1963">
<h3><a name="page-1963">Wednesday, March  8, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben &amp; Josie started<span class='line-break'> </span> to the hospitle at Charlottsville.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am distressed about Josie. Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she may come back improved.<span class='line-break'> </span> J Jim split wood in the<span class='line-break'> </span> woods and got wood and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> it in for us to burn. The<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynols come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening. I milked<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning &amp; to night. The first<span class='line-break'> </span> time in several weeks. The cow<span class='line-break'> </span> kicked at me but did not<span class='line-break'> </span> hurt me much. Max can<span class='line-break'> </span> come tonight to see his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother. Jim Doss carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin Smith a load of straw.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wish I could see all of <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins folks and him two.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1964">
<h3><a name="page-1964">Thursday, March  9, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. Rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Max Car went from here<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Jim went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Lee Brumfields to a <span class='line-break'> </span> cutting match. Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey come to see us<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. She eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner with us. Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie come home today from <span class='line-break'> </span> Charlottsvill. We was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to have them back. Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> is feeling bad I know.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went <span class='line-break'> </span> to school. Hattie Gilbert<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today. Most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the clothes was dry enough<span class='line-break'> </span> to take in. Oh how I<span class='line-break'> </span> wish I could See Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> folks. It rains rains rains.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1965">
<h3><a name="page-1965">Friday, March 10, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day. Rained all night<span class='line-break'> </span> last night and it is raining to<span class='line-break'> </span> night. They teacher intended to<span class='line-break'> </span> have a box party at the school<span class='line-break'> </span> houes tonight but I guess there<span class='line-break'> </span> wont be many there. I am sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that the weather is so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben has not done much<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Henry &amp; Edna went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had caned sausage &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> eggs and tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed dishes after<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and fixed the<span class='line-break'> </span> butter. Have not done much<span class='line-break'> </span> today except dodge around<span class='line-break'> </span> and set by the fire.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben milked Lady tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie milked Red.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1966">
<h3><a name="page-1966">Saturday, March 11, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Clear most of the day. Cool<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; windy. Ben &amp; Jim cut<span class='line-break'> </span> and sawed up the wood that<span class='line-break'> </span> the ice broke and cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> up the spring yard. The nicest<span class='line-break'> </span> it has bin in along time.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they did it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has tried to see what<span class='line-break'> </span> she could do today. She helped<span class='line-break'> </span> to milk then cut salit for <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Went to the spring &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> washed it. Killed a chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> and dressed it. Finished<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner then baked a cake. Washed<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel &amp; Franklin and dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> them. Helped milk tonight and got<span class='line-break'> </span> up the eggs. Washed the dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> after supper. I kept busy but <span class='line-break'> </span> did not do much of any thing.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1967">
<h3><a name="page-1967">Sunday, March 12, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day. Josie &amp; I <span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner. Mrs Car washed <span class='line-break'> </span> dishes. I would of liked <span class='line-break'> </span> to go some where but could <span class='line-break'> </span> not well go. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have felt bad &amp; lonesome<span class='line-break'> </span> all day and no prospect<span class='line-break'> </span> of any thing better. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1968">
<h3><a name="page-1968">Monday, March 13, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> put on the plantbed canvas<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Lee &amp; Oscar come<span class='line-break'> </span> here today to see a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> buying some feed. They eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner with us. Miss <span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Wooding come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening &amp; Ila &amp; Cordie Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> and Nettie Hendricks and<span class='line-break'> </span> her little baby. The baby <span class='line-break'> </span> is a beauty. I think Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> made a bed quilt lineing<span class='line-break'> </span> and put a quilt in the <span class='line-break'> </span> frames today and we quilted<span class='line-break'> </span> more than half of it. Cordie<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Isla &amp; Miss Willie all<span class='line-break'> </span> quilted some. Edna has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sick today. She could not go<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1969">
<h3><a name="page-1969">Tuesday, March 14, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Rained a little and cleared<span class='line-break'> </span> off. Jim &amp; Ben went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> and cut wood for Irvin Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve oclock. They come<span class='line-break'> </span> home for dinner. They worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> the garden fence this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We quilted one of Josies quilts<span class='line-break'> </span> and commenced on another one.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs. Norman Booker come and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>helped us quilt</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Kate Harvey &amp; Carrie Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while. Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> had four of the children with<span class='line-break'> </span> her. I was so glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them. Would be glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Paul &amp; Roy. Hope to <span class='line-break'> </span> see all of them soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car has bin sick all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening hope she will get well soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1970">
<h3><a name="page-1970">Wednesday, March 15, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning. Clear tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben worked on the <span class='line-break'> </span> garden this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry &amp; Edna went to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and [?] finished Josies <span class='line-break'> </span> quilt and put one in the <span class='line-break'> </span> frames. I quilted a little <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Car is quite sick <span class='line-break'> </span> yet. I do hope she may be<span class='line-break'> </span> better by morning. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim found five little pigs<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday morning. We are<span class='line-break'> </span> very glad of them &amp; hope <span class='line-break'> </span> to rais them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1971">
<h3><a name="page-1971">Thursday, March 16, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some corn this morning &amp; <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the stalks to the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> then worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cut a <span class='line-break'> </span> nice mees of <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> up today. Mollie Reynols was<span class='line-break'> </span> here today a little while.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> helped us <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> some. We <span class='line-break'> </span> finished the quilt tonight. That<span class='line-break'> </span> is three that we have quilted <span class='line-break'> </span> this week. <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> Harvey is <span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight he brought us <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>. We are mighty<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to get it. Nine oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> and bed time I think.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1972">
<h3><a name="page-1972">Friday, March 17, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben &amp; Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the garden fence <span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning. This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> they helped cut wood <span class='line-break'> </span> at Mag Brumfields. They <span class='line-break'> </span> went on the car. I went <span class='line-break'> </span> with them. I went to Kates <span class='line-break'> </span> and then we went to Mags.<span class='line-break'> </span> I saw Doris &amp; Virginia &amp; Hellen. <span class='line-break'> </span> They all looked very nice. <span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner at home. <span class='line-break'> </span> We had turnip salit. We<span class='line-break'> </span> have had good neighbors to <span class='line-break'> </span> send us salid. Hattie Gilbert <span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today. Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> baked a cake today as nice <span class='line-break'> </span> as one could wish. Mag <span class='line-break'> </span> had a very nice dinner today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I eat some with her this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1973">
<h3><a name="page-1973">Saturday, March 18, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> cloudy day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> on his plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed until twelve. He come <span class='line-break'> </span> home to <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Gretna. Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with him.  Jim went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>. I done some shopping.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben bought some <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> got home about night.  <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and Professer Gambol went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the Sulpher Strings.  <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come here. Henry &amp; Hugh went <span class='line-break'> </span> down the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not catch any thing.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie Gravely</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> this evening. We<span class='line-break'> </span> were very glad that she come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did want to go and see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1974">
<h3><a name="page-1974">Sunday, March 19, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We all staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cooked <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7809' title='greens'>greens</a> and a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> stewed <a href='../subjects/7746' title='prunes'>prunes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> baked. Josie is <span class='line-break'> </span> feeling mighty bad today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I said we all staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I forgot <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> home with <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> did not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Wilson Starkey<span class='line-break'> </span> got stuck in the mud<span class='line-break'> </span> near the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went &amp; helped him<span class='line-break'> </span> get out.  I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7959' title='letters'>letters</a> today. One to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; one to Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson.  Wish I could see them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1975">
<h3><a name="page-1975">Monday, March 20, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy morning. Colde and<span class='line-break'> </span> windy tonight. Ben put the wire<span class='line-break'> </span> a round the flower garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I hope to enjoy planting<span class='line-break'> </span> things in the garden. I put a quilt <span class='line-break'> </span> together and Josie put one together<span class='line-break'> </span> and made a lineing. Josie got <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Mrs Car washed dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned. We put a quilt<span class='line-break'> </span> in the frames. All of us quilted<span class='line-break'> </span> a square. Ben quilted a few<span class='line-break'> </span> lines. Jim come home this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Nellie went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie today. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she did. I want to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her so bad but I cant go.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has bin pent today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1976">
<h3><a name="page-1976">Tuesday, March 21, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8444' title='Benjami Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> garden <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day. It is so <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>cold</a> they quit<span class='line-break'> </span> before night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> churned this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning &amp; washed dishes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> milked.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We quilted a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning. I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all quilted this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think most of the folks<span class='line-break'> </span> have gone to bed so that<span class='line-break'> </span> they can get warm.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> scool (crossed out) school. <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> got a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7297' title='Virginia Owen?'>Virginia</a> wood (crossed out)<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1977">
<h3><a name="page-1977">Wednesday, March 22, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde day.  Ben &amp; Jim cut <span class='line-break'> </span> some wood in the woods. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry &amp; Edna went to school. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie milked. Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> churned.  I got breakfast and <span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes and got dinner &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> supper. Josie &amp; Mrs Car and I <span class='line-break'> </span> quilted some. We finished <span class='line-break'> </span> the quilt tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Hattie &amp; Elie washed to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I tried to bring a chunk <span class='line-break'> </span> of fire from the parlor to <span class='line-break'> </span> my room and droped it. <span class='line-break'> </span> Burnt the drugget &amp; the <span class='line-break'> </span> floor. I am sorry but it <span class='line-break'> </span> cant be helped now. <span class='line-break'> </span> I will not try such a thing <span class='line-break'> </span> a gain soon if ever. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1978">
<h3><a name="page-1978">Thursday, March 23, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9272' title='clear cool'>clear cool</a> day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> firmed up the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Ben hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> this evening. Jim <a href='../subjects/9261' title='split wood'>split <span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> in the woods. Clay Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come here a bout [day?] this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning on his way to <a href='../subjects/9273' title='Lynchburg'>Lynchburg</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got some gas from Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> His had gave out. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9240' title='ironed'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some and got dinner. Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car had the <a href='../subjects/9274' title='sick headache'>sick headache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I put a <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> in the frames<span class='line-break'> </span> all by my self. <span class='line-break'> </span> We all <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a> on it this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynolds come<span class='line-break'> </span> and helped us. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she come. Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> come and went with her<span class='line-break'> </span> home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1979">
<h3><a name="page-1979">Saturday, March 25, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> land. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/9265' title='Renan'>Renan</a>. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9240' title='ironed'>ironed</a> all the morning. Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car <a href='../subjects/9241' title='churned'>churned</a>. Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner in 30 minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had <a href='../subjects/9266' title='caned sausage'>caned sausage</a><span class='line-break'> </span> made a <a href='../subjects/9267' title='dewberry pie'>dewberry pie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> had <a href='../subjects/9268' title='caned tomatoes'>caned tomatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> boiled 14 <a href='../subjects/9269' title='egg'>egg</a> made <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a>. <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come &amp; <a href='../subjects/9270' title='Carrie'>Carrie</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> children. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see all of them. Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; I worked <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate brought some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9271' title='sallit'>sallit</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1980">
<h3><a name="page-1980">Sunday, March 26, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> fixed the<span class='line-break'> </span> gate to the <a href='../subjects/7785' title='flower garden'>flower garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were glad to have it made so<span class='line-break'> </span> we could go in the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> moved his <a href='../subjects/453' title='pig'>pig</a> to the<span class='line-break'> </span> pasture today. Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> went home this evening. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went. They did not go in at<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Powers. Most all of the<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers people are <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a>. I <span class='line-break'> </span> heard a gun shot tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> We heard that a mad <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was killed. S[h]ot near<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee Brumfields.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There has bin more passing<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout today than any Sun[day]<span class='line-break'> </span> since Xmas. Looks like<span class='line-break'> </span> rain now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Chris Tenigs Reynols was here today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1981">
<h3><a name="page-1981">Monday, March 27, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<a href='../subjects/9263' title=' Jim'> Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> and had to quit. The<span class='line-break'> </span> land got too wet. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> made a <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> lineing<span class='line-break'> </span> and we put in a quilt.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a snack for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a> a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then went to Mr Bookers.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ruth Brookers mother was<span class='line-break'> </span> there Mrs Jackson. I<span class='line-break'> </span> liked her fine for the<span class='line-break'> </span> acgiatanice[acquaintance]. Josie is <a href='../subjects/9264' title='feeling bad'>feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> bad</a> tonight I am so sorrie<span class='line-break'> </span> for her. Jim found the <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> nests today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1982">
<h3><a name="page-1982">Tuesday, March 28, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9228' title='rainy'>rainy</a> day. There was a <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cloud this morning and this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Ben and Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> some between <a href='../subjects/9262' title='showers'>showers</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> tied the <a href='../subjects/9246' title='cow'>cow</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a fraid she would kill her<span class='line-break'> </span> self and he untied her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> has felt mighty bad today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I don't feel well. Oh at the<span class='line-break'> </span> trouble I see about that that<span class='line-break'> </span> cant be helped. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a> some this evening &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. Irvin Harvey come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening and brought us some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9254' title='salit'>salit</a>. I was glad of it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bob Starkey wants to rais a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to morrow.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1983">
<h3><a name="page-1983">Wednesday, March 29, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/9261' title='split wood'>split wood</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some today. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>barn raising</a> at Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Elders on Bob Starkeys<span class='line-break'> </span> land.  Did not get home<span class='line-break'> </span> until night.  <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>. The other one<span class='line-break'> </span> we could not do any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> with. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> in several weeks.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nat Wooding brought us<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/9254' title='salit'>salit</a> to day. We were<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of it. Denia Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> today. She come to see Mrs Bookers<span class='line-break'> </span> She was not at home and<span class='line-break'> </span> she come here. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1984">
<h3><a name="page-1984">Thursday, March 30, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day. <a href='../subjects/9260' title='Rained'>Rained</a> some &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a>. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> a round some when it was not<span class='line-break'> </span> raining.  <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. She has a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> in the frames. I did very<span class='line-break'> </span> common. I went to Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields and spent the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a pleasand day. Grace<span class='line-break'> </span> had a good dinner. John &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Edwin Brumfield was there at<span class='line-break'> </span> work on the porch. Os(crossed out) Oscar<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come for me and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me home. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to go but hated to leave.<span class='line-break'> </span> So much for Josie to do.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie come with us home<span class='line-break'> </span> but did not get out of the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got some flowers.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1985">
<h3><a name="page-1985">Friday, March 31, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Another rainy day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> worked some when it<span class='line-break'> </span> was not raining. Ben helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a> a bout his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7903' title='stable'>stable</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin Smith came down for<span class='line-break'> </span> feed. He eat dinner with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all so glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> him. John &amp; Edwin Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace come with them.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all so glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> finish quilting<span class='line-break'> </span> on her <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a>. I bound it this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Hattie <a href='../subjects/9256' title='washed'>washed</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> day. They did not get dry.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want it to get<span class='line-break'> </span> clear so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1986">
<h3><a name="page-1986">Saturday, April  1, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde windy day.<a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='Mill'>Mill</a> at <a href='../subjects/7522' title='Level Run, Virginia'>Level Run</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>. He went with <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/9257' title='Gretna'>Gretna</a>. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> worked a<span class='line-break'> </span> round the house all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Mr. Woodings<span class='line-break'> </span> and got some <a href='../subjects/9258' title='turnip salit'>turnip salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner. She has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin very [pert?pent] to day and I<span class='line-break'> </span> am glad. I <a href='../subjects/9259' title='hemed'>hemed</a> one <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today. We all went to Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker's this evening. Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Jackson and Mrs Less<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers was there. We had<span class='line-break'> </span> a pleasant evening. It is <span class='line-break'> </span> so colde tonight that we<span class='line-break'> </span> have fire like winter time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1987">
<h3><a name="page-1987">Sunday, April  2, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day. We<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins and eat dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> had a time to crank<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> but finely did get<span class='line-break'> </span> it to go. We had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> trip concidering the bad roads.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie was not looking for<span class='line-break'> </span> us but had a plenty<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  They had a lot of<span class='line-break'> </span> company. John and his wife &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> daughter Mr and Mrs Hodges Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Love &amp; children Christinia &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Floyed Reynols.  We got home<span class='line-break'> </span> in time to do our work. Mr Kent<span class='line-break'> </span> come and hindered <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a>. He did<span class='line-break'> </span> not milk one of the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>. Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Kent is <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a> with <a href='../subjects/9205' title='flue'>flue</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim got home tonight I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that he come tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1988">
<h3><a name="page-1988">Monday, April  3, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/9252' title='sowed'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9253' title='clover seed'>clover seed</a>. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> got rock off<span class='line-break'> </span> the new ground. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. She cut <a href='../subjects/9254' title='salit'>salit</a> and <a href='../subjects/9255' title='stewed peaches'>stewed <span class='line-break'> </span> peaches</a>. I put a <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> frames. We both <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. We both <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. I milked the cow <span class='line-break'> </span> that kickes so some times. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie <a href='../subjects/9256' title='washed'>washed</a> the clothes <span class='line-break'> </span> dried and we took them in. <span class='line-break'> </span> Gladice Brumfield come <span class='line-break'> </span> with the children from <span class='line-break'> </span> school. Franklin Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> and Alvin Mayhew stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> at Mr Booker and stayed<span class='line-break'> </span> an hour or more this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1989">
<h3><a name="page-1989">Tuesday, April  4, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some with a double <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plow</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed some in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>. <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped them some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> all but <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and she cried most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning. Tonight she was good.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9250' title='starched'>starched</a> her clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a snack except<span class='line-break'> </span> make the bread. Josie done<span class='line-break'> </span> that. Josie <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> we both <a href='../subjects/9251' title='quilted'>quilted</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben quilted some tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin <a href='../subjects/7626' title='reading'>reading</a> when <span class='line-break'> </span> I should of bin in bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am olde eneough to do better.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1990">
<h3><a name="page-1990">Wednesday, April  5, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/9229' title='plowed'>plowed</a> under<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a>. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> plowed some in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> and planted <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and I finished<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilting</a>. Josie <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/9246' title='cow'>cow</a> kicked her and<span class='line-break'> </span> hurt her leg. Ben milked<span class='line-break'> </span> that cow tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished two of Josies<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9247' title='quilts'>quilts</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Mable some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/210' title='drawers'>drawers</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has cried a lot<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I think that<span class='line-break'> </span> something hurts her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Norman Booker traded<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Three of the children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1991">
<h3><a name="page-1991">Thursday, April  6, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked in the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> pickin up and burning <span class='line-break'> </span> brush as long as they could<span class='line-break'> </span> and not get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a>, I worked the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> and put on<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/33' title='buttons'>buttons</a>. I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I finished<span class='line-break'> </span> three <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilts</a>, that is all<span class='line-break'> </span> of them ready to use.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1992">
<h3><a name="page-1992">Friday, April  7, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
