<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day no rain. <a href='../subjects/8444' title='Benjami Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim worked in the orchard<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaning up. <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> had a <a href='../subjects/443' title='colde'>colde</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; did not go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> came a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning would<span class='line-break'> </span> not stay for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/9245' title='vines'>vines</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> the porch this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to [Renan]<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>. He come <span class='line-break'> </span> home <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>. Hope he will<span class='line-break'> </span> be well by morning. I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> Lady <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1993">
<h3><a name="page-1993">Saturday, April  8, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the Island</a> to Pat <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Woodings</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for two <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He come home by eleven<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked corn</a>. They finished<span class='line-break'> </span> shucking &amp; hauled it to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/285' title='corn house'>corn house</a>. It was dark<span class='line-break'> </span> when they come with the<span class='line-break'> </span> last of it. Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had fresh <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> breakfast &amp; dinner. Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow. I killed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>hen</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We hope that <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>'s<span class='line-break'> </span> folks will come. I am a<span class='line-break'> </span> fraid it will be raining.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1994">
<h3><a name="page-1994">Sunday, April  9, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Cloudy but no rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> some in their fancy <a href='../subjects/9244' title='gardens'>gardens</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> I got most of the  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> cleaned up<span class='line-break'> </span> the house and she made the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a> for dinner. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomson &amp; family come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us.  And <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> family all in the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them<span class='line-break'> </span> all. <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; Jamie &amp; Gladice<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield &amp; Christina<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while. They did not come in <span class='line-break'> </span> the house. They played with<span class='line-break'> </span> the children while they<span class='line-break'> </span> staid.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1995">
<h3><a name="page-1995">Monday, April 10, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A nice day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> gardened <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in the rye. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; I went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We carried some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and two bushel of <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Solde them all to Mr.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rucker. Bought<span class='line-break'> </span> several things and come <span class='line-break'> </span> home and left most of them<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>. I am very<span class='line-break'> </span> much bothered about<span class='line-break'> </span> leaving them. Cordie Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see her. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and all of <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> one of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>. Today is <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jims</a> birth day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1996">
<h3><a name="page-1996">Tuesday, April 11, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/287' title='windy'>windy</a> day and some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee and Oscar come and got two<span class='line-break'> </span> loads of <a href='../subjects/8262' title='corn stalks'>corn stalks</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> orchard today. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> made<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7748' title='hot bed'>hot bed</a> to day and<span class='line-break'> </span> worked in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> half<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. <a href='../subjects/9204' title='Mabel'>Mabel</a> has a bad<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/443' title='colde'>colde</a> and is so cross that<span class='line-break'> </span> we cant hardly stand her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> has <a href='../subjects/9242' title='sewed'>sewed</a> some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I fixed some on my <a href='../subjects/9243' title='chicken coops'>chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> coops</a> and <a href='../subjects/9242' title='sewed'>sewed</a> on my<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a> a little. I have wrote<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie a letter to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Now it is time that we<span class='line-break'> </span> was in bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1997">
<h3><a name="page-1997">Wednesday, April 12, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very good day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/9229' title='plowed'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> cleaned up the<span class='line-break'> </span> land for Ben to plow. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> plowed a little after he come<span class='line-break'> </span> from school. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/9240' title='ironed'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. I <a href='../subjects/9241' title='churned'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George Blairs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia was not at home<span class='line-break'> </span> she had gone to Rey<span class='line-break'> </span> Worshams. Ethel has a new<span class='line-break'> </span> boy. I hope that Ethel &amp; baby<span class='line-break'> </span> may get on well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry Blair was at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> He brought me home on<span class='line-break'> </span> his new <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>. I was glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cant walk much now<span class='line-break'> </span> like I once could. I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> of any kindness that is given to me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1998">
<h3><a name="page-1998">Thursday, April 13, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/9229' title='plowed'>plowed</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben <a href='../subjects/9238' title='ditched'>ditched</a> the <a href='../subjects/9236' title='spring branch'>spring <span class='line-break'> </span> branch</a>. <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all day his birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day. He is six years olde today. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> ironed all the morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. Josie sewed <span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening. I sewed <span class='line-break'> </span> on my <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a>. Will be glad <span class='line-break'> </span> when I get it done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I <a href='../subjects/9239' title='milked'>milked</a> morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1999">
<h3><a name="page-1999">Friday, April 14, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> ditched on the <a href='../subjects/9236' title='Spring Branch'>Spring <span class='line-break'> </span> Branch</a>. The school children <span class='line-break'> </span> come home at twelve oclock. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> got dinner. I sewed <span class='line-break'> </span> on my <a href='../subjects/9202' title='quilt'>quilt</a>. I finished it. <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to [Mount Airy] this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I washed up the <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner dishes while they <span class='line-break'> </span> were gone. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a> yet. <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blains</a> to go <a href='../subjects/9237' title='gigin'>gigin</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> This is first trip of that <span class='line-break'> </span> sort. I hope that nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> wont happen to him. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am worried about things <span class='line-break'> </span> in spite of knowing I should <span class='line-break'> </span> be thankful that things is no worse.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2000">
<h3><a name="page-2000">Saturday, April 15, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished the <a href='../subjects/9234' title='ditch'>ditch</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> cleaned out the <a href='../subjects/9235' title='springhouse'>springhouse</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim plowed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> little. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. Together we<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner then I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Reynols's. Bruce is at<span class='line-break'> </span> home. He brought Mollie <span class='line-break'> </span> some of the nices <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> I most ever saw.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Christenia was colering<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> for Easter. Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> was fixing his tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> land. Jim set one<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> today. Hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> the others will set<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2001">
<h3><a name="page-2001">Sunday, April 16, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. No rain yet. <span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> all day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> worked on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> some. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Robert &amp; Reubin Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that they <span class='line-break'> </span> come. They would not <span class='line-break'> </span> stay for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> &amp; I got dinner. We <span class='line-break'> </span> had a <a href='../subjects/9233' title='roast hen'>roast hen</a> and a<span class='line-break'> </span> very  nice <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and not <span class='line-break'> </span> much besides.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am glad that all are well as we are.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2002">
<h3><a name="page-2002">Monday, April 17, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy cool day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> plowed all day. <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> up the branch in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school. Come home at noon <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Ben and Josie and all of<span class='line-break'> </span> the children went to <a href='../subjects/9225' title='Mount Airy'>Mount Airy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to a spelling bee. I staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home a while. Norman Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; family went to <a href='../subjects/9226' title='Level Run'>Level Run</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and to Jim Bookers fish trap. <span class='line-break'> </span> They had a fish fry. It was very<span class='line-break'> </span> nice much better than I expected.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was a crood there and all<span class='line-break'> </span> seemed to enjoy the sport.<span class='line-break'> </span> Norman Bookers <a href='../subjects/9232' title='horse'>horse</a> got cut<span class='line-break'> </span> in the wire fence yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do so much thank them<span class='line-break'> </span> for taking me with them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2003">
<h3><a name="page-2003">Tuesday, April 18, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and a little rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> worked most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day. The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school. <a href='../subjects/8489' title='Franklin'>Franklin</a> has a <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>cold</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> &amp; I got a snack for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Josie washed<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes. I went to <a href='../subjects/9227' title='Renon'>Renon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and to see Kate Harvey.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a pleasant evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I walked there and<span class='line-break'> </span> back. Some thing I won't <span class='line-break'> </span> do many more time without <span class='line-break'> </span> a change. I have to do so<span class='line-break'> </span> much hard work here <span class='line-break'> </span> that I can't get no rest<span class='line-break'> </span> and then don't do half<span class='line-break'> </span> eneough to suit them<span class='line-break'> </span> that I do for.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2004">
<h3><a name="page-2004">Wednesday, April 19, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9228' title='rainy'>rainy</a> day &amp; <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a>. A bad day<span class='line-break'> </span> on little chickens. The men<span class='line-break'> </span> could not work much. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Edna went to school today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I got a snack for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Johnson Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> come as we was ready for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. He eat with us.I<span class='line-break'> </span> was glad that he did. I have<span class='line-break'> </span> not worked on anything to<span class='line-break'> </span> day like sewing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie is not well. She has<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/443' title='colde'>colde</a> and says she feels<span class='line-break'> </span> so sad. I hope that she may<span class='line-break'> </span> soon feel better. She helped<span class='line-break'> </span> me <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2005">
<h3><a name="page-2005">Thursday, April 20, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked on a peice of<span class='line-break'> </span> new ground all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/9231' title='Edna'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> is complaining<span class='line-break'> </span> to night. Hattie Gilbert<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie found her pin that<span class='line-break'> </span> she lost a week or so<span class='line-break'> </span> ago. I am miserable.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is so much that<span class='line-break'> </span> is needing to be done and<span class='line-break'> </span> no one much able to do.<span class='line-break'> </span> And them that could be<span class='line-break'> </span> so much help is not<span class='line-break'> </span> willing but there will<span class='line-break'> </span> be some sort of a way<span class='line-break'> </span> provided for the children.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2006">
<h3><a name="page-2006">Friday, April 21, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning. <a href='../subjects/187' title='Cloudy'>Cloudy</a> and some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening. <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and some of the children <span class='line-break'> </span> are very much complaining. <span class='line-break'> </span> Think they have the <a href='../subjects/9205' title='flue'>flue</a>. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin in bed nearly all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Henry went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come home and went to the store.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got some <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>. Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaned them ready for breakfast.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on his new ground<span class='line-break'> </span> all morning. <a href='../subjects/9229' title='Plowed'>Plowed</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I have done what<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9230' title='cooking'>cooking</a> was done and not<span class='line-break'> </span> much besides.  I know I <span class='line-break'> </span> dont do what I might but<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout all that I am<span class='line-break'> </span> able to do.  I want to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and the children so bad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2007">
<h3><a name="page-2007">Saturday, April 22, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the time and some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8487' title='Ben'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a> both <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie creeps about but<span class='line-break'> </span> should be in bed. The<span class='line-break'> </span> children all have <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went home this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I hope that he may<span class='line-break'> </span> come home alright.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8427' title='Henry'>Henry</a> done the feeding tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to Mr Bookers<span class='line-break'> </span> and got some flour.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mollie and Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols come a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> for me. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to get it off.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2008">
<h3><a name="page-2008">Sunday, April 23, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day so cold that<span class='line-break'> </span> I am afraid it will frost<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Ben and Josie has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sick all day. They come to the<span class='line-break'> </span> dining room tonight. I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that they will soon be better<span class='line-break'> </span> and that none of the rest will<span class='line-break'> </span> get sick. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> came home ok.<span class='line-break'> </span> He eat dinner at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that he did. Wish I<span class='line-break'> </span> could of bin there two. He<span class='line-break'> </span> came with Faber and Paul and<span class='line-break'> </span> Alma part of the way home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that he did get to<span class='line-break'> </span> come that way. Oh when I get<span class='line-break'> </span> to thinking about all of the<span class='line-break'> </span> children. I want to see them<span class='line-break'> </span> so bad but cant go and they wont come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2009">
<h3><a name="page-2009">Monday, April 24, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> and <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> [day].There was <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> enough to kill some things.  I think it killed most of our <a href='../subjects/9203' title='strawberry blooms'>strawberry blooms</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to the island for <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a> this evening he <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> is sick and <a href='../subjects/9204' title='Mabel'>Mabel</a>. They<span class='line-break'> </span> all have <a href='../subjects/9205' title='flue'>flue</a> we think.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to school.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> have done what cooking has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin done.  Milked this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight Josie helped.  I know she<span class='line-break'> </span> should not do as much as<span class='line-break'> </span> she does.  Hattie washed here<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I am distressed<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout them all being <a href='../subjects/9206' title='sick'>sick</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I cant do what is needing<span class='line-break'> </span> to be done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>

<div id="page-2010">
<h3><a name="page-2010">Tuesday, April 25, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool day some <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning Tim has plowed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has tried to work this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. Him &amp; Josie are some better<span class='line-break'> </span> of their cough. I do hope that they all<span class='line-break'> </span> may get well soon. Henry is not<span class='line-break'> </span> well tonight. I do hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> all will soon be well. Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franklin went to the store<span class='line-break'> </span> today for beef &amp; salmon. Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> come by from school and got<span class='line-break'> </span> coffee &amp; corn flakes. I wrote two<span class='line-break'> </span> letters and got one today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I put out fifteen little<span class='line-break'> </span> chickens this evening. Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> got out some nails that was in<span class='line-break'> </span> old paleings to build a coop<span class='line-break'> </span> to put the <a href='../subjects/9207' title='hen'>hen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in.</p>

<div id="page-2011">
<h3><a name="page-2011">Wednesday, April 26, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day Ben &amp; Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Henry did not go to<span class='line-break'> </span> school the first day he has<span class='line-break'> </span> missed this [seccion?session]. The baby<span class='line-break'> </span> has cried the most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is not well. I got a<span class='line-break'> </span> letter from Carrie today. I<span class='line-break'> </span> am always glad to hear from<span class='line-break'> </span> them. I have bin sick all<span class='line-break'> </span> day but not so [bad] but I could<span class='line-break'> </span> go until about night. I could<span class='line-break'> </span> not get supper. Hope I will<span class='line-break'> </span> soon be better. All has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sick some but Jim. I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope he may not get sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> We got the first greens<span class='line-break'> </span> from the plant bed today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad we will have<span class='line-break'> </span> plenty soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2012">
<h3><a name="page-2012">Thursday, April 27, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day the most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks cold not do much<span class='line-break'> </span> work. They worked some<span class='line-break'> </span> between showers.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Josie milked this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and tonight. Josie has done<span class='line-break'> </span> the cookin. I have sick all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Hope I will soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be well as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mabel come to my bed and <span class='line-break'> </span> got in and went to sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> the first time in her life<span class='line-break'> </span> that I know of.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2013">
<h3><a name="page-2013">Friday, April 28, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day rained most of<span class='line-break'> </span> day. I dont know what the <span class='line-break'> </span> men folks did not much of any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing I guess. Josie worked<span class='line-break'> </span> about all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have bin in bed the<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day am so sick<span class='line-break'> </span> that I can hardly sit up.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today was [Dinas ?] birthday.</p>
</div>

<div class="page-content">

</div>

<div id="page-2015">
<h3><a name="page-2015">Sunday, April 30, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clean cool day. There was<span class='line-break'> </span> frost this morning. Not enough <span class='line-break'> </span> to [hunt?] much. We all have<span class='line-break'> </span> bein at home all day. There<span class='line-break'> </span> has not any one come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us in about two weeks.<span class='line-break'> </span> [Reylein?] Reynolds came to<span class='line-break'> </span> see me today. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that he came.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie has bin [busy?] about<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. She cooked meat +<span class='line-break'> </span> greens and baked a cake,<span class='line-break'> </span> milked and churned. Kept<span class='line-break'> </span> Busy about all day. I<span class='line-break'> </span> hope I can help her some<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow. [Nonny?] is not well<span class='line-break'> </span> by no means. Alma Bennett<span class='line-break'> </span> called over the [thove?]. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she did. She was on her way home</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2016">
<h3><a name="page-2016">Monday, May  1, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim worked the <span class='line-break'> </span> Garden this morning Ben planted <span class='line-break'> </span> some mellons then went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the School House to Speakin [crossed out] <span class='line-break'> </span> Speaking.  Ben eat Dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> at Johnsons to day was [Rauly?] <span class='line-break'> </span> Birth day he eat Dinner at <span class='line-break'> </span> Home he was 22 years olde today. <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie was Sick last night. <span class='line-break'> </span> She got up and got Breakfast. <span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin up all day but <span class='line-break'> </span> did as little as I could. <span class='line-break'> </span> heard today that Marvin is <span class='line-break'> </span> sick hope he may Soon be <span class='line-break'> </span> well I want to See them all <span class='line-break'> </span> so bad. The Boys [commenced?] <span class='line-break'> </span> to plant corn this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope the Weather will <span class='line-break'> </span> stay good a while. </p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2017">
<h3><a name="page-2017">Tuesday, May  2, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Irvin Hervey was <span class='line-break'> </span> here today. he eat Dinner here. <span class='line-break'> </span> he come [fo?] Seed corn. Denia <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us today I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see her. I got a letter <span class='line-break'> </span> from Carrie today. Marvin [wry?] <span class='line-break'> </span> out trying to work. Josie [ironed?] <span class='line-break'> </span> and starched today will <span class='line-break'> </span> have a big ironing to morrow. <span class='line-break'> </span> I got Dinner went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> plant seed for [salit?]. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to <span class='line-break'> </span> School then Henry &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> store got home at dark. <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry brought a jug of <span class='line-break'> </span> [ail?] I was glad he got <span class='line-break'> </span> it. </p>

<div id="page-2018">
<h3><a name="page-2018">Wednesday, May  3, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

I got a bushel of meal <span class='line-break'> </span> and paid [Hulebard?] what we <span class='line-break'> </span> owed him. The men could <span class='line-break'> </span> not do much today. Ben killed <span class='line-break'> </span> three crows. Josie and I got a <span class='line-break'> </span> snack for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Mabel a pair<span class='line-break'> </span> of drawers. I worked the<span class='line-break'> </span> button holes in them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sewed a little on any <span class='line-break'> </span> guilt did not get it done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-2019">
<h3><a name="page-2019">Thursday, May  4, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

I finished <span class='line-break'> </span> the squares for a quilt <span class='line-break'> </span> we don't have much <span class='line-break'> </span> trouble cooking not much <span class='line-break'> </span> to cook.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school one of the Mayhew <span class='line-break'> </span> children got sick at <span class='line-break'> </span> school and they had to <span class='line-break'> </span> send for him <span class='line-break'> </span> I wrote [cousine] a letter.</p>

<div id="page-2020">
<h3><a name="page-2020">Friday, May  5, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day not much rain. Ben &amp; [Booker] went to the [wlang] for [guano] they got home about two o'clock. Jim worked on his new ground. Josie cut Salit for dinner. I done the cooking Josie I [?oned] Fate Harvey came to see us and Mrs. Booker &amp; two little children. Then Mollie Reynolds come ( was glad to see them all do hope that the weather [?] will soon get good.  Today was Eva Smiths birth day. She is four. I want to go there to see them all so bad.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-2021">
<h3><a name="page-2021">Saturday, May  6, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A day that did not rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys hauled wood<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the store for beef and soda.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went to Jessie Hutcherson <span class='line-break'> </span> for oil. There is a play<span class='line-break'> </span> at the school house tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> [ho?] one went from here<span class='line-break'> </span> [orvin?]. Harvey was here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening for some [salit?}<span class='line-break'> </span> Alvin Farmer was with him<span class='line-break'> </span> on a car. Josie has worked<span class='line-break'> </span> all day cleaning up and making<span class='line-break'> </span> beds. she baked a nice cake<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. I have bin up<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day but did<span class='line-break'> </span> not do much of anything.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hived some bees this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they will stay here and work.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2022">
<h3><a name="page-2022">Sunday, May  7, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home alday. Been and family<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr. Towers this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I went to Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers this evening. They had<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of company. Mr. and Mrs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dave Booker was there. Otho and <span class='line-break'> </span> Sallie and George and Ida and [carchie?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair and I went up there a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs. Booker called and invited<span class='line-break'> </span> me. I enjoyed seeing them all.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come home and milked and<span class='line-break'> </span> fed the chickens<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mabel is sick tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope she may be well<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning. I hope that all<span class='line-break'> </span> may get well and stay so<span class='line-break'> </span> a while.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2023">
<h3><a name="page-2023">Monday, May  8, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day Fanny Tower<span class='line-break'> </span> come last night. She was<span class='line-break'> </span> with us at Breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben Brought <span class='line-break'> </span> to [Onarins?] Smiths when<span class='line-break'> </span> we got here Carrie &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> the children had gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> [Renan] we mised them Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> found the peice of the <span class='line-break'> </span> drill that they thought <span class='line-break'> </span> was lost. Carrie said <span class='line-break'> </span> that Josie had milked<span class='line-break'> </span> all of the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel worried a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> so much to do<span class='line-break'> </span> and I am not helping.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2024">
<h3><a name="page-2024">Tuesday, May  9, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day I got Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> to go to town. and do some <span class='line-break'> </span> shopping for me this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> She mailed some of the <span class='line-break'> </span> things to Josie I [staid] <span class='line-break'> </span> with the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had [salit] and <span class='line-break'> </span> Straw Berries for Dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Carrie and I <span class='line-break'> </span> picked about five gallons<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie sent some of <span class='line-break'> </span> her neighbors some and <span class='line-break'> </span> will preserve the rest<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the creek but <span class='line-break'> </span> could not find anywhere <span class='line-break'> </span> to fish [neese?] got me a <span class='line-break'> </span> pen &amp; ink to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2025">
<h3><a name="page-2025">Wednesday, May 10, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9394' title='good'>good</a> morning. had a<span class='line-break'> </span> Thunder cloud this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and a very hard rain. <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come Home at noon to take us<span class='line-break'> </span> to Galveston to see <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a>. the rain come so <span class='line-break'> </span> we could not go. I <a href='../subjects/9120' title='plucked'>picked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Straw berries most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> preserved <span class='line-break'> </span> some of them. Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> made a part of a little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8079' title='suit'>suit</a> for <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> to be in a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> at the <a href='../subjects/968' title='Straight Stone school'>School House</a><span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/9418' title='John'>John</a> or <span class='line-break'> </span> any of his folks yet hope to<span class='line-break'> </span> see them soon<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to know what they <span class='line-break'> </span> are doing at Home so <a href='../subjects/9351' title='bad'>bad</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Hope they are getting on ok. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2026">
<h3><a name="page-2026">Thursday, May 11, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day Carrie finished<span class='line-break'> </span> Roys suit this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> she killed a chicken for <span class='line-break'> </span> Dinner I dressed it I<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some Straw Berries<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Carrie and the <span class='line-break'> </span> little girls and I to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie and her folks all <span class='line-break'> </span> of the Family and Frances<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; her Baby was there<span class='line-break'> </span> Alma &amp; Gordon &amp; Frances <span class='line-break'> </span> intends to go to Danville <span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning<span class='line-break'> </span> I an anxious to hear <span class='line-break'> </span> from home have not seen <span class='line-break'> </span> John yet want to <span class='line-break'> </span> go there tomorrow if<span class='line-break'> </span> I can. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2027">
<h3><a name="page-2027">Friday, May 12, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/9394' title='good'>good</a> day. <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some Tobacco</a>. <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9256' title='washed'>washed</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> She got done before 10<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock then she <a href='../subjects/9400' title='killed'>killed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/9354' title='chicken'>chicken</a> for Dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>Straw<span class='line-break'> </span> Berries</a> and [cpp] capped<span class='line-break'> </span> them we had all that we <span class='line-break'> </span> could eat &amp; some to<span class='line-break'> </span> Preserves<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to see <a href='../subjects/9418' title='John'>John</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Tenia</a>. We eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with them John has a <span class='line-break'> </span> nice house we [w??]<span class='line-break'> </span> [Turnished?] I think we <span class='line-break'> </span> got home a bout Dark<span class='line-break'> </span> now we are ready for the Bed.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2028">
<h3><a name="page-2028">Saturday, May 13, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2029">
<h3><a name="page-2029">Sunday, May 14, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  Carrie and the children come with me Home.  Josie had a nice [Dri?].  Josie is [handily?] able to go a bout  Lee &amp; Hilda spent the day with us.  [Jeanine ?] Power went home [sic] but came back again tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is wrote on Monday and was [Siel?] last night and forgot to write.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2030">
<h3><a name="page-2030">Monday, May 15, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys [hunted?] cut worms most of the day.  Mr Mayhew helped them get off some big rocks.  Josie got dinner this evening.  She went to the plant bed and cut salit for dinner tomorrow. Tonight she is broke down.  Went to bed.  Did not eat supper.  I have [bin?] up most of the day.  I churned this morning and milked two cows this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wrote two letters this morning one to Willie &amp; one to Carrie. [Henry?][?] worked on Edna a [Do?] to day.  The children went to school.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2031">
<h3><a name="page-2031">Tuesday, May 16, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day no rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> their Tobacco land all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. Franklin staid<span class='line-break'> </span> with the men all day the<span class='line-break'> </span> first time in his life.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner and [churn?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has lein sick all<span class='line-break'> </span> day. Mollie Reynolds come<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening. I<span class='line-break'> </span> was glad she come. I<span class='line-break'> </span> milked to night. Fanny<span class='line-break'> </span> Power made bread and coffee<span class='line-break'> </span> for supper. I had a <span class='line-break'> </span> letter from Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith to day. I wish<span class='line-break'> </span> I could hear from them<span class='line-break'> </span> every day</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2032">
<h3><a name="page-2032">Wednesday, May 17, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very rainy day the men could not work the children did not go to school.  Josie has been sick all day. She served some </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2033">
<h3><a name="page-2033">Thursday, May 18, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rainy morning. quit<span class='line-break'> </span> about twelve Ben + Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some tobacco the<span class='line-break'> </span> children choped ptants<span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry planted some carie<span class='line-break'> </span> Sent a piece of goods to make<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel a chess. Kate + Joace <span class='line-break'> </span> come This evening on Lees<span class='line-break'> </span> buggy I was glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come Fannie made Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> a dress today Farmie milk<span class='line-break'> </span> the red cow this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> + tonight that is a gmea<span class='line-break'> </span> help to one she coasties<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> Jose has begin wh doing today<span class='line-break'> </span> oft that she could get<span class='line-break'> </span> well again </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2034">
<h3><a name="page-2034">Friday, May 19, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clean cool Day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2035">
<h3><a name="page-2035">Saturday, May 20, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> worked in the garden some<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning. This evening Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> went home. Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> him to [Gaetna?]. Henry &amp; Frank<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him. He bought<span class='line-break'> </span> a nice fish at [Gaetna?]. We<span class='line-break'> </span> had all we could eat at<span class='line-break'> </span> supper &amp; some left. I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the plant bed<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning for lettice.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Johnson brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie &amp; Kate Hubbard and Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> Jr. Jane and [?] Jr. they <span class='line-break'> </span> are two fine little boys.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come. Tonight Josie walked<span class='line-break'> </span> one cow &amp; Fanny [Tower?] milked<span class='line-break'> </span> one &amp; I milked one.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2036">
<h3><a name="page-2036">Sunday, May 21, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Fannie [?] went<span class='line-break'> </span> to [preaching?] to day will come<span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight. Jim come home<span class='line-break'> </span> allright all of [Maraines?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Family and Himself come<span class='line-break'> </span> with Him. I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them all Mrs. Gravely<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Josie this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Otho and Sellie Blain [?] Ruth<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker come this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Mr. Booker and Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went to look for<span class='line-break'> </span> StrawBerries did not find<span class='line-break'> </span> any worth gathering<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] had fried chicken for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner the firts that has<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] raised this year. Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> made a cake this morning</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2037">
<h3><a name="page-2037">Monday, May 22, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim &amp; Ben have worked on Tobacco land today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Frannie Power was here. This morning also a man by the name of Lony. his car went […] on him and he could not get it to go so he come and ask to stay alright he got it fixed some time today. Josie &amp; Franny went and got some […] for Dinner. I have worked more in the garden today than any time this year and felt as well as usual. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2038">
<h3><a name="page-2038">Tuesday, May 23, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim + Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on their Tobacco land. Henry +<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna went to School. I got <span class='line-break'> </span> Dinner. Tommie washed dishes <span class='line-break'> </span> after Dinner. Mrs Kent<span class='line-break'> </span> come she brought us some <span class='line-break'> </span> nice cabbage she wanted to<span class='line-break'> </span> swap some eggs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Isla + Cordie Blair come to<span class='line-break'> </span> See us this evening. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad they came. Mabel has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin good today for her to be.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fannie made Mabel a Dress<span class='line-break'> </span> to day a pink gingham she<span class='line-break'> </span> is proud of it.<span class='line-break'> </span> After supper to night Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Cor + Ella Hubbard +<span class='line-break'> </span> Ron Hubbard come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Posie. I am glad that they came to see her</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2039">
<h3><a name="page-2039">Wednesday, May 24, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The men folk<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on tobacco land all day Mrs. [Car-?] and Ela spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day with Josie. Mr Sam Hubbard came for Ella.<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Anna and little [Louise?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbard came with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Anna brought Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> some light bread. Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds came late this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening we had the cabbag<span class='line-break'> </span> that Mrs Kent brought<span class='line-break'> </span> and lettice and ham for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. I got a letter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Carrie today. I am<span class='line-break'> </span> always glad to hear from<span class='line-break'> </span> her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2040">
<h3><a name="page-2040">Thursday, May 25, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. The boys <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their Tobacco land all day<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted some potatoe slips<span class='line-break'> </span> Today Josie &amp; fanny got <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. They killed chickens <span class='line-break'> </span> and cooked cabbage.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert &amp; Louis <span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Hutcherson &amp; mrs Evylin <span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherso &amp; Ada Hutcherso <span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were on mrs Hutcherson's <span class='line-break'> </span> car. Ada was driving <span class='line-break'> </span> the car. I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that they come. Evylin's <span class='line-break'> </span> baby is a fine fellow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2041">
<h3><a name="page-2041">Friday, May 26, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day we had a shower<span class='line-break'> </span> The men planked some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this evening. Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin suffering all day<span class='line-break'> </span> today. Fannie ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> of the clothes and starched <span class='line-break'> </span> the others I got up the<span class='line-break'> </span> turkeys. I sent and<span class='line-break'> </span> got a half bushel of<span class='line-break'> </span> meal from Jessie Hutchens<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to get it. I<span class='line-break'> </span> finished plantting potatoe<span class='line-break'> </span> slips this morning. I am <span class='line-break'> </span> so glad I did.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fannie helped me milk <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight. She got supper<span class='line-break'> </span> She is washing dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight Josie [_orped?] them<span class='line-break'> </span> She would not let [mms came?]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2042">
<h3><a name="page-2042">Saturday, May 27, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy cool day the most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day. Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> They planted some after dark<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie are uneasy a<span class='line-break'> </span> fraid the children will<span class='line-break'> </span> be sick from the work. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> was mad or something he<span class='line-break'> </span> would not eat any supper<span class='line-break'> </span> They think they are [onost?]<span class='line-break'> </span> two good to work at any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing hard. Some one has to<span class='line-break'> </span> work to keep the rest idle<span class='line-break'> </span> I know I am nothing but<span class='line-break'> </span> a slave an not looked on<span class='line-break'> </span> as any thing more. While <span class='line-break'> </span> some can and does sit &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> ly around and are [reveransed?]<span class='line-break'> </span> like a queen.  Guess that is allright<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2043">
<h3><a name="page-2043">Sunday, May 28, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very cool day for the last<span class='line-break'> </span> of May. We need rain so they<span class='line-break'> </span> people can finish planting <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco. Ben &amp; Norman [Booker?]<span class='line-break'> </span> walked a round some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning then Ben carried [mms]<span class='line-break'> </span> Car to Mr. Towers. They come <span class='line-break'> </span> here for dinner then thay <span class='line-break'> </span> started to Charlottsvill. I <span class='line-break'> </span> hope they got there ok.  Wish <span class='line-break'> </span> I knowed about them<span class='line-break'> </span> Reubin &amp; Robbert &amp; Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jane Reynolds come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us a while this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Asa Anderson come to thake<span class='line-break'> </span> Frannie Power home. I will<span class='line-break'> </span> miss Fannie. We found Jims <span class='line-break'> </span> turkey here tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2044">
<h3><a name="page-2044">Monday, May 29, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. Jim plowed the<span class='line-break'> </span> garden and planted some seed<span class='line-break'> </span> of one kind or other. Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> has not come home yet. Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey come a while. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she come. We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the cherrie tree &amp; curant<span class='line-break'> </span> bush. Kate tolde me that<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomas Thomson &amp; Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvin Smiths<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school. Hattie washed here<span class='line-break'> </span> Today I borrowed soap from<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Booker paid it back<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. I keep going<span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep and blot my <span class='line-break'> </span> book.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2045">

<div class="page-content">

Ben &amp; Josie &amp; Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car come home this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to have them<span class='line-break'> </span> at home but so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that the Dr could not<span class='line-break'> </span> help her in some way<span class='line-break'> </span> The [?] school closed<span class='line-break'> </span> today. I am glad to have the<span class='line-break'> </span> children at home a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Mrs. Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  Mrs Edmons<span class='line-break'> </span> stoped a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; [Lizzie?] and [Loraine?]<span class='line-break'> </span> and Frances &amp; Shirley &amp; [Cary?] <span class='line-break'> </span> Jefferson come by from<span class='line-break'> </span> the Red House. I was glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> see them. I dropped some ink <span class='line-break'> </span> an made a mess of it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2046">
<h3><a name="page-2046">Wednesday, May 31, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> tonight and<span class='line-break'> </span> a little rain. <a href='../subjects/8496' title='Jim'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and <a href='../subjects/7641' title='feed cutting'>cut</a> off <a href='../subjects/8435' title='ordering tobacco'>tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hills getting aready to plant<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice Thomson</a> &amp; children<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8086' title='Jennie Owen'>Mrs</a> Thomson &amp; I and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> to white falls. We<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch</a>  many <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a><span class='line-break'> </span> but had a good time. Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car was with <a href='../subjects/8488' title='Josie'>Josie</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and the little girls<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while. <a href='../subjects/7297' title='Virginia Owen?'>Virginia</a> H and <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> B come a a while. The<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to the Sulpher<span class='line-break'> </span> Springs. They had a good time<span class='line-break'> </span> Their <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>teachers</a> was with them.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.</p>

<h3><a name="page-2048">Friday, June  2, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Josie has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> some better today. I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner. Mrs. Car churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and washed dishes. I will be so glad when<span class='line-break'> </span> we can get vegetables a plenty.</p>
