<div id="page-2120">
<h3><a name="page-2120">Sunday, August 13, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and a little<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  We all staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked snaps &amp; corn &amp; chicken.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Made apple dumplings and one<span class='line-break'> </span> damson pie.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; the children and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car went to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers and to see Mrs Trent.<span class='line-break'> </span> She would not come with<span class='line-break'> </span> them home.  I wanted her<span class='line-break'> </span> to come but dont think<span class='line-break'> </span> hard of her.  I would not if<span class='line-break'> </span> I was in her position.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim brought some fine<span class='line-break'> </span> water mellons to the house<span class='line-break'> </span> He cut two.  They were<span class='line-break'> </span> very good.  I made coffee &amp; baked <span class='line-break'> </span> bread for supper.  No one eat much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2121">
<h3><a name="page-2121">Monday, August 14, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> A good rain tonight.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks helped Norman Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> cut tobacco.  All of them <span class='line-break'> </span> got wet.  Had two loads of<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to hoist tonight so had<span class='line-break'> </span> supper late.  Edna &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> brought in some wood &amp; brought <span class='line-break'> </span> water and put up the milk<span class='line-break'> </span> while I milked the cows.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace &amp; Effie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Josie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They brought some apples.  I am glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Claud &amp; Nellie Hendricks<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I was glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> they did.  I ironed a little <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys have some fine mellons.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2122">
<h3><a name="page-2122">Tuesday, August 15, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Rain tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks finished cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> a [c...ing?] of tobacco for<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker &amp; commence to cut for<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben.  Irvin Harvey &amp; [Aulens?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield helped them cut.<span class='line-break'> </span> Norman &amp; a little nero [negro?]helped<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  They did not fill the <span class='line-break'> </span> barn.  Carrie &amp; her <span class='line-break'> </span> children come a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Max can come home this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning eat dinner here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight there is a gathering <span class='line-break'> </span> at Lee's and [M...?]<span class='line-break'> </span> went.  I am [m....?]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2123">
<h3><a name="page-2123">Wednesday, August 16, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben finished cutting tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> enough to fill his barn.<span class='line-break'> </span> They suckered tobacco this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to the barn <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Josie has suffered<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot today.  No one come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see her today.  I think she<span class='line-break'> </span> was glad.  I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and caned 8 cans of<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes.  I am afraid they <span class='line-break'> </span> wont keep.  We have some <span class='line-break'> </span> of the finest tomatoes I ever <span class='line-break'> </span> saw.  I guess the rainy<span class='line-break'> </span> time will ruin them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben went to Renon <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Did not stay many<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  I got supper this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> while I canned tomatoes. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2124">
<h3><a name="page-2124">Thursday, August 17, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> suckered tobacco until twelve<span class='line-break'> </span> then worked on the barns.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> rode around trying to get help.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not get any one. Ben is at<span class='line-break'> </span> the Barn tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> [Clifton?] &amp; Jane and the boy &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Thelma Brunmfield come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see Josie today.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them. I was at the <span class='line-break'> </span> kitchen getting dinner. Jane<span class='line-break'> </span> peeled the potatoes &amp; mashed<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Mrs Car &amp; I peeled a <span class='line-break'> </span> few tomatoes &amp; I caned <span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I walked a lot today<span class='line-break'> </span> looking for a cow and did<span class='line-break'> </span> not find her.  Jim found her<span class='line-break'> </span> and a little calf.  Ben helped <span class='line-break'> </span> me get her in the stall.<span class='line-break'> </span>   </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2125">
<h3><a name="page-2125">Friday, August 18, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben fined<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.  Jim sowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some turnip see[d] this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Mills and his <span class='line-break'> </span> hands worked the road to <span class='line-break'> </span> day and put in a new<span class='line-break'> </span> bridge.  Queen[ie] Callans<span class='line-break'> </span> washed for us today the <span class='line-break'> </span> first time.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  I cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> turnip [salit?] the first I <span class='line-break'> </span> ever cooked in August.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynols &amp; Thelma<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield walked here<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Johnson &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Reubin come for Molly<span class='line-break'> </span> in the car.  Thelma<span class='line-break'> </span> staid all night here.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that she did.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2126">
<h3><a name="page-2126">Saturday, August 19, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  Rain this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening very hard.  The branch<span class='line-break'> </span> was out of its banks.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the Cork Mill this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  He got his wheat <span class='line-break'> </span> ground.  Got home at dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Franklin went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  Thelma went from<span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening and walked<span class='line-break'> </span> through the mud.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the snap [pa.els] and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> snaps and some sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes.  Think I will make<span class='line-break'> </span> some pies in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Thelma ironed some this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2127">
<h3><a name="page-2127">Sunday, August 20, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hugh &amp; [?]&amp; Ernest<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry there.  Dave Booker come<span class='line-break'> </span> he was on a car. They all<span class='line-break'> </span> got on it and went to Lees.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  I cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> snaps and chicken baked<span class='line-break'> </span> sweet potatoes made pies.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The first potatoes of this<span class='line-break'> </span> season.  No one come to <span class='line-break'> </span> see us today. [I] would of <span class='line-break'> </span> bin glad for some one to<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  This is a plentiful<span class='line-break'> </span> year of vegetables and fruit<span class='line-break'> </span> I have had some thing to<span class='line-break'> </span> cook that is nice most evry<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I want to be thankful.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2128">
<h3><a name="page-2128">Monday, August 21, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim cut his first<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco today.  Evry body around<span class='line-break'> </span> was cutting today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner then started<span class='line-break'> </span> to Renan.  Met Mrs Hutcherson[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Miss Ada. They going to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons ask me to go and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went.  I was glad to go.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> cut some nice water mellons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Hutcherson &amp; Ada Brough<span class='line-break'> </span> me to Renan.  I was going <span class='line-break'> </span> to see KAte Harvey.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> was gone to [Allaw..a?] so I <span class='line-break'> </span> come by Mollies.  She had ice<span class='line-break'> </span> cream.  Gave me a sauser<span class='line-break'> </span> full.  She come with me nearly<span class='line-break'> </span> home and brought some ice<span class='line-break'> </span> for Josie.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2129">
<h3><a name="page-2129">Tuesday, August 22, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim finished<span class='line-break'> </span> filling the barn with tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening They cut for Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Booker.  Thelma spent the <span class='line-break'> </span> day here.  I was glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> have her.  Cordie Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  She brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie some pretty flowers.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Cordie.  I wish they all would<span class='line-break'> </span> come often.  Josie has suffered<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot today.  I am so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> for her and cant do anything<span class='line-break'> </span> to help her.  I went for<span class='line-break'> </span> snaps this evening.  Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> has strung them.  Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> milked one cow this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She can be so much help<span class='line-break'> </span> when she will.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2130">
<h3><a name="page-2130">Wednesday, August 23, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> helped Norman Booker finish cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco today.  Jim is fineing<span class='line-break'> </span> his tobacco to night.  Queen <span class='line-break'> </span> Callans washed for us today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has bin feeling bad<span class='line-break'> </span> all day. Mollie REwnols<span class='line-break'> </span> come today.  Johnson brought<span class='line-break'> </span> her &amp; come after her.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I ironed some today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The children has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to bed &amp; sleep.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> about asleep.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has some fine water <span class='line-break'> </span> mellons.  I have not felt <span class='line-break'> </span> well today.  Hav not eat <span class='line-break'> </span> vegetables or fruit all day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Do hope I may be well<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2131">
<h3><a name="page-2131">Thursday, August 24, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning rain tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben moved two cureings of <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Jim is fineing his.<span class='line-break'> </span> Queen Callans ironed here <span class='line-break'> </span> today. Ellen Lewes &amp; Lilly <span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She brought Josie some<span class='line-break'> </span> sanwitches[sic].  Josie has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> feeling bad all day.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> carried some goods to <span class='line-break'> </span> make Franklin some<span class='line-break'> </span> [...ants].<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not felt well<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I kept up but it<span class='line-break'> </span> was all that I could do.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some snap<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2132">
<h3><a name="page-2132">Friday, August 25, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim fined tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben &amp; Henry helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Booker move tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> When the men come to <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner Rufus &amp; Max Car <span class='line-break'> </span> come with them.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> snaps &amp; peas for dinner. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Josie. <span class='line-break'> </span> I starched the clothes <span class='line-break'> </span> that needed it then ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening,  Did not <span class='line-break'> </span> get done.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2133">
<h3><a name="page-2133">Saturday, August 26, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on the tobacco until twelve. <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I to <span class='line-break'> </span> White Falls.  I fished some.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Caught four little fish.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> river was very mudy.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> had bin all out of the <span class='line-break'> </span> banks.  Mr Johnson &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Roach[?] was at work to <span class='line-break'> </span> get the things out that had <span class='line-break'> </span> washed in the mill so <span class='line-break'> </span> that they could not grind.<span class='line-break'> </span> Sarah &amp; Billie Emerson <span class='line-break'> </span> come to night.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Sarah. We had <span class='line-break'> </span> turnip salit for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2134">
<h3><a name="page-2134">Sunday, August 27, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then Ben &amp; Jim went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.  Ben went for<span class='line-break'> </span> medicine.  They went to <span class='line-break'> </span> see Marvin &amp; Carrie.  Nellie <span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvin's.  They got <span class='line-break'> </span> home about night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Sarah &amp; Billie Emerson<span class='line-break'> </span> went home late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope they got there safe.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner all but <span class='line-break'> </span> the bread.  Sarah made<span class='line-break'> </span> and baked the bread.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car washed the dishes<span class='line-break'> </span> after breakfast &amp; Sarah <span class='line-break'> </span> churned while I milked<span class='line-break'> </span> the cows gathered snaps <span class='line-break'> </span> and killed chickens.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2135">
<h3><a name="page-2135">Monday, August 28, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks moved some tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; cut some.  They cur <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry's crop.<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Anna Hubbard and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Ella &amp; Baby come to <span class='line-break'> </span> see Josie today.  They got<span class='line-break'> </span> here a bout eleven o'clock.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Josie.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went and gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> snaps for dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Some of them strung<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Well I am a <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep.  Will go to bed<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2136">
<h3><a name="page-2136">Tuesday, August 29, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> cut tobacco.  Finished cutting <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben's and commenced on <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim's.  Miss and Ela <span class='line-break'> </span> went home early this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked snaps &amp; potatoes <span class='line-break'> </span> and chicken and made<span class='line-break'> </span> apple dumplings.  Josie had <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Hutcherson and Herbert<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey &amp; Virginia &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Hellen Brumfield &amp; Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols.  Johnson come for <span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie.  Queen Callans <span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.  I want <span class='line-break'> </span> to see Carrie so bad <span class='line-break'> </span> but cant go any where <span class='line-break'> </span> to stay any time. </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2137">
<h3><a name="page-2137">Wednesday, August 30, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men cut <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.  They are <span class='line-break'> </span> hoisting some now &amp; at <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  No one come today. <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie suffered most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  I got snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; butter beans for<span class='line-break'> </span> denner.  I went and <span class='line-break'> </span> gathered peas and got <span class='line-break'> </span> some sweet potatoes <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the water mellon<span class='line-break'> </span> patch for the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> since it was planted.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hatties children come<span class='line-break'> </span> for apples.  Say they will <span class='line-break'> </span> dry some.  They may.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-2138">
<h3><a name="page-2138">Thursday, August 31, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They finished <span class='line-break'> </span> cutting tobacco here today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad.  Norman Booker <span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner with us.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening Mrs Edmons &amp; [...?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham stopped in to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie.  Mr Jenning come in a<span class='line-break'> </span> a while to see her.  I did <span class='line-break'> </span> not see them.  I was gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to get snaps.  While I was <span class='line-break'> </span> gone Lawson &amp; Fannie <span class='line-break'> </span> Power come.  They are gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Renan to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Irvin Harvey is going to <span class='line-break'> </span> have a [tea?] at the <span class='line-break'> </span> barn and some of his <span class='line-break'> </span> friends will be with <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  I hope they will enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span> The [asseesor?] was here today.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-2139">
<h3><a name="page-2139">Friday, September  1, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> both have tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> in the barns.  They will <span class='line-break'> </span> stay at the barns tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to [Carrie?]<span class='line-break'> </span> and got a girl to come <span class='line-break'> </span> and stay with us <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Mrs Car went <span class='line-break'> </span> to them to the island.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She bought several <span class='line-break'> </span> things.  I went to Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest.  I fished a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I caught 6 fish.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> fried them for Josies <span class='line-break'> </span> supper.  Nat Wooding<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; wife &amp; Mrs Peak <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Josie today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Max is here tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-2140">
<h3><a name="page-2140">Saturday, September  2, 1922</a></h3>

<div id="page-2141">
<h3><a name="page-2141">Sunday, September  3, 1922</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim has staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn all day.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> has tried to start the [engine?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Posie &amp; [Clack?] come and <span class='line-break'> </span> helped him this evening but they <span class='line-break'> </span> could not get it to work <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Kellie &amp; Lottie Kellie<span class='line-break'> </span> come here this evening. Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Booker come. Nellie &amp; Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Marvin &amp; children come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> A coloured girl &amp; I got <span class='line-break'> </span> the dinner.
